Finally, he reported on the victory in suppressing bandits. The initial work of suppressing bandits has shown effectiveness. The second step of the rural cleansing work has now begun. The spirit of suppressing bandits must be used to cleanse the countryside, restore and ensure local peace and order. (29th Special Dispatch)

National Army Captures Yihuang

(Nanchang) On the 26th, the National Army went straight to the city of Yihuang and bravely besieged it. At 11 am on the 27th, they captured the city of Yi. The bandits broke through the encirclement and fled south. (29th Special Dispatch)

Wang Jun Handles the Aftermath in the Bandit Areas of Western Anhui

(Xuzhou) Military news: Regarding the aftermath in the bandit areas of western Anhui, Wang Jun has telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Government to form an aftermath committee to handle the recruitment of refugees and the reorganization of local militias. However, due to the extremely rapid military progress, there is a lack of aftermath funds. Wang has appointed personnel from the Third Army Headquarters and the party departments of the Seventh and Twelfth Divisions to take charge of the handling, and has telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Government to quickly send cadres to take over and reorganize the political affairs. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Road report: Wang Jun's proclamation restores order in the recovered areas, prohibits revenge and retaliation, and protects the private property of the people. Refugees have been returning to their homes one after another, and order has been restored. However, these areas have been communistized for four years, and many land and property deeds have been destroyed. In the future, boundary disputes may be unavoidable. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Military News: Many bandits were killed in western Anhui. More than 500 hostages were rescued, all of whom were gentry and merchants kidnapped from Zhengyangguan, Liu'an, Huoshan, and Huoqiu. They have now been sent back to their hometowns separately. The remaining bandits are fleeing towards Dushan. It is expected that the bandit atmosphere in Anhui can be eliminated. (29th Special Dispatch)

Plot Exposed, Twenty-Seven People Arrested

(Jinan) The Qingzhou Communist Party's plan to riot after the autumn harvest was detected by the county government and the provincial party department. The Communist Party gathered seventy or eighty people, fired guns, and surrounded the Zhengmu Township District Office to seize weapons. The Yidu County Magistrate immediately led a team to disperse them, capturing more than ten leaders, including Ji Huchen, the principal of the town's elementary school. Yesterday, the headquarters sent an armored car, and the provincial party department sent Wang Tiansheng to Qingzhou. This morning, more than ten people were arrested in various schools, for a total of twenty-seven people. They were escorted to Jinan today. It was found that the Communist Party had incited farmers, schools, and local militias. Now that the roster and plans have been seized, they can be rounded up in one fell swoop to prevent trouble before it happens. The locals are celebrating. This is the first time that the Communist Party has fired guns and rioted in this province. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Ma Ze Zhao, the representative of Xikang stationed in Beijing, said that the Kang-Tibetan issue could be resolved peacefully, which is what the people hope for. It is difficult for the Dalai Lama to end the matter on this basis. In terms of military strength, there are 20,000 Tibetan soldiers in the front. It is now appropriate to take advantage of the opportunity to occupy Ping Qiang Du in order to defend it. Otherwise, we are still afraid of withdrawing from Dege. Foreign Important Telegrams

Bleak Clouds Loom Over the Future of Japanese Politics

The Seiyukai's Attitude Suddenly Turns Harsh

Refusal to Compromise with the Government on Rescue Measures

Prime Minister Saito Finds it Difficult to Please Everyone

Navy Minister Okada Runs Around Attempting to Mediate

Emergency Parliament Decides to Extend Session by Three Days

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 29th - Prime Minister Saito is striving to break the deadlock regarding the debt restructuring plan and the Rice Law amendment, but the Seiyukai is maintaining a firm stance, saying there is no room for compromise. Within the cabinet, members from the Seiyukai, such as Finance Minister Takahashi and Railway Minister Mitsuchi, are firmly opposed to the debt restructuring plan, while Agriculture Minister Goto is adhering to his own views regarding the Rice Law amendment, threatening to resign. The government absolutely opposes both plans, putting it in a very difficult situation. As a result, the government may make mutual concessions with the Seiyukai and persuade Agriculture Minister Goto to yield, in an attempt to find a compromise and turn the situation around. However, this will depend on Prime Minister Saito's actions. Conflict is unavoidable, and the situation is quite serious.

▲ China United Press, Tokyo, 29th - The Japanese political situation is at a standstill due to the Seiyukai's proposal of the Rice Law amendment, the Debt Restructuring Association Law, and the Central Bank Law, which conflict with the government's proposals. Initially, it was reported that the Seiyukai leaders had compromised with the government, causing unrest among the radicals within the Seiyukai. Today, a joint meeting was held in the afternoon to discuss countermeasures, and it was decided that no concessions would be made on the above three proposals. The meeting adjourned at 10:30 PM. Meanwhile, the Minseito party also held an emergency meeting within the Diet, resolving to oppose the Seiyukai's three proposals and fully support Agriculture Minister Goto, without proposing alternative bills. The government, due to Agriculture Minister Goto's insistence on opposing the Seiyukai's proposals, also decided within the cabinet to support Goto. With such a stalemate, conflict is unavoidable. Saito dispatched Navy Minister Okada to meet with Budget Committee Chairman Okada, entrusting him with the task of easing the opposition. Later, he consulted with Mori Kaku, and Railway Minister Mitsuchi also visited Mochizuki Keisuke to smooth things over with the opposition within the Seiyukai. However, the outcome is not yet optimistic.

▲ China United Press, Tokyo, 29th - The Japanese emergency parliament has decided to extend its session by three days, scheduled to end on September 2nd. If the issues cannot be resolved by then, it will be extended again to the 4th. The Minseito, Seiyukai, and Kokumin Domei parties have all expressed criticism, saying that if the government continues in this manner, even extending the session by ten days will be futile. The Seiyukai, in particular, held a meeting of its executives, urging the government to immediately accept the Rice Law amendment, debt restructuring, and Central Bank Law proposed by the party. Otherwise, they are prepared to initiate a vote of no confidence. The Japanese political situation is becoming increasingly serious.

Air Combat Exercises in Tokyo on the 1st of Next Month

▲ China United Press, Tokyo, 29th - Tokyo City has organized the Imperial Capital Defense Corps, divided into fifteen districts, specifically as an air defense organization in wartime. The members of each corps are mainly from youth groups and retired soldiers. The mayor of Tokyo has been appointed as the joint leader of the defense corps. Air raid and air defense drills are scheduled for September 1st. The aircraft participating in the air combat include bombers from the Army's Tokorozawa unit, student aircraft from the Student Aviation League, and a dozen or so civilian aircraft.

Wu Teng Narrowly Escapes Assassination Twice Before Going to the Northeast

▲ According to the Osaka Asahi Shimbun, at 3:35 PM on the 21st, when Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary Wu Teng was at Kyoto Station before his departure, there was a large crowd seeing him off. Police officers and military police were on high alert. Unexpectedly, a suspicious-looking man was discovered in the third-class waiting room. Upon searching him, officers from the Shichijo police station found a six-shot pistol in his possession, intending to harm Wu Teng. The man, named Kintaro Kitamura, resided in Konyacho, Kanda Ward, Tokyo. Fortunately, he was arrested on the spot, and disaster was averted. Also, on the 23rd, when Wu Teng left Kyoto heading west on passenger car No. 101, an obstruction suddenly occurred as the train passed east of Todō Station in Tsuno County, Yamaguchi Prefecture. The driver braked sharply and saw a large granite boulder of over a foot in size placed across the tracks and guard rails, narrowly avoiding a derailment. The Tokuyama police station considered the matter serious and launched a rigorous search for the perpetrator.

Papen Criticizes the Nazi Party

Resolves to Suppress Political Violence with Force

His Rash Actions Disqualify Him from Holding Political Power

Also Explains Economic Reform Plan

Issuing Tax Credit Certificates to Open Up New Sources of Revenue

Incentivizing Private Enterprises to Reduce Unemployment

▲ Reuters, Berlin, 29th - In a radio address yesterday, Prime Minister Papen, after criticizing the National Socialist Party, stated that Germany cannot abandon its global economic relations and adopt autarky. The cabinet also supports autonomy, but only to the extent of providing essential food supplies. Therefore, the cabinet will continue to implement moderate import management methods. As for the monetary system, it must not be endangered, the mark must not be devalued, and private businesses must not be interfered with. Germany's recovery plan involves expanding public works and restoring private enterprises to absorb the unemployed. 130 million marks can be allocated for public works, and 2 billion marks can be risked to boost industry. The National Bank has already agreed to this. Taxes that hinder production, such as transaction taxes, estimated to amount to 1.3 billion marks next year, will be returned to economic life in the form of certificates. Taxpayers can use these to borrow an equivalent amount from the National Bank. The government also plans to loan 700 million marks to businesses that increase employment. Wages can be reduced to a minimum, and official salaries must also be reduced. This plan has been decided to be implemented for one year. Papen's final remarks indicated that he has no intention of resigning. He said, "I believe it is my responsibility to resist all improper interference from party forces. The next few months will be devoted to settling matters. The rash behavior of Nazi leader Hitler following the Büssen murder trial shows that he is not qualified to be a government leader. As for the current cabinet, it will crack down on the activities of the National Socialist Party. If necessary, I will use force to extinguish the fires of civil war and eliminate political violence."

▲ Nationalist News Agency, Berlin, 29th - German Chancellor Papen stated in a speech at the Westphalia Farmers' Congress today: (1) The government hopes to provide jobs for 1.75 million unemployed people through its economic reform plan; (2) The current government will never disregard the fundamental principles of the Weimar Constitution; (3) He and his cabinet members will never allow any party to seize political power by depriving others of their rights. Regarding the economic reform portion, Papen strongly emphasized the importance of the domestic market, arguing that progress in the domestic market is a prerequisite for improving the national economic life. However, it is also important not to endanger export trade. The government has never considered interfering in private enterprises because it wants to build new confidence in the future of the German economy and must re-stimulate the spirit of private enterprise. The government's unemployment reduction plan aims to incentivize private businesses to increase their employment. One of the biggest obstacles at present is that many factories have neglected factory repairs and renovations in recent years due to a lack of capital. To provide the necessary capital, the government will work closely with the Deutsche Bank to issue tax credit certificates, based on transaction taxes, transportation taxes, and land taxes, etc., which are due in October 1933. In the future, these certificates can be used to pay a portion of taxes, but income tax cannot be paid with these certificates. The issuance will be discounted, and is thus effectively a loan. The government hopes to raise 1.5 billion marks through this, of which 700 million marks will be used to incentivize the hiring of new employees. The plan is to subsidize employers with 400 marks in tax credit certificates for each new employee hired each year. If these 700 million marks can be fully utilized, they should be able to provide jobs for 1.75 million unemployed people. Further details regarding the government's plan will be announced when the government outlines its policy direction to the new parliament. He wants to solemnly declare that the government will never disregard the fundamental principles of the Weimar Constitution, nor will it ever consider changing the republican government.

▲ Havas, The Hague, 29th - The Anti-Imperialist War Conference continued today. The Danish representative said that fascism is emerging in various countries and expressed resistance. He believes that the conference is a way to oppose war. The representative of the French Revolutionary Minority Party of the Second International declared that the minority party of French socialism is strongly opposed to imperialist war. Number of Russian Red Guards Increases

Mostly from the Farmer-Worker Class

▲ Nationalist News Agency, Moscow, 28th - New recruits will join the Red Guards on September 1st, all strong men born in 1910, reaching the age of military service, and conscripted for training. According to the Pravda newspaper, the Red Guards are increasing every year, and the percentage of soldiers from the worker and peasant classes is also increasing year by year. An investigation showed that in 1927, soldiers from the worker and peasant classes accounted for only 23.8% of the Red Guards, but this year it has reached 35.5%. 55% of the Red Guard soldiers are Communist Party members or Communist Youth League members. As for the officers, in the past year alone, 300 field officers and captains joined the party, as well as more than 20,000 non-commissioned officers. All recruits are thoroughly reviewed, and only those whose political views and other qualifications are not contrary to the party are allowed to join. Among the worker and peasant classes, only those who strictly adhere to communism are entrusted with the important task of defending the country.

Imprisonment of a Spanish Rebel General

Where is the Spirit of His Former Heroism?

▲ Havas, Santoña, Spain, 28th - The Dueyasso penal colony is where General Sanjurjo is being held to atone for his crimes. The penal colony is located in the province of Santoña. The prison building is isolated from the outside world, with over a hundred guards armed with guns standing guard outside. To reach the prison, journalists must pass through several high stone walls and undergo layers of interrogation before reaching the courtyard of the prison. Finally, they arrive at room number 52, where Sanjurjo is detained. The furnishings of the cell are simple, consisting of a cabinet, a table, a chair, and an iron bed. Sanjurjo has received special treatment from the authorities, so the iron bed is covered with a wool mattress. The small cabinet contains the clothes that Sanjurjo wore during his battles in Morocco, recalling the time when Sanjurjo wore these clothes, full of spirit and unrivaled. Now, however, he guards this iron window for the rest of his days. The room has a small window facing the sea, with the sea crashing against the jagged rocks below. Sanjurjo wears a gray prison uniform with yellow markings. There is a vase of flowers and several books on the table. The general seems to be quite healthy. When someone talks about his new life, the general replies, "[I hope to get used to it soon and put all the worries behind me. Although I am currently ill, the only thing that occupies my mind is my family.]" It is said that when Sanjurjo first arrived, the prisoners here were greatly stimulated, because Sanjurjo used to come to inspect them when he was the commander of the security forces.

Lion Enters City, No One Injured

▲ Fixed Nationalist News Agency, Warsaw, 28th - A lioness was discovered today in the city of Kielce, Poland, in the middle of a busy street. Pedestrians who suddenly saw the lioness frantically ran to avoid it, but the lioness, as if it knew the way, slowly walked towards the park, without looking around or disturbing anyone. After entering the park, it slowly lay down on the grass, relaxed and at ease. Later, after gathering many police officers and soldiers armed with weapons to surround it, a lion tamer entered and led the lioness into a cage, which was transported back to the circus. It turned out that the lioness was a trained lion from a certain circus and had accidentally escaped, causing the scare.

There was no mention of the military authorities. Special telegram for investigation and correction. Yan Yin, Business Department, Ministry of Railways.

Conditions of Self-Defense Army's Anti-Japanese Resistance Under Feng

Talks from a Returned Guest from Jilin

A communication from Beiping states that a person who recently came from Jilin spoke in great detail about the recent anti-Japanese conditions of the Self-Defense Army under Feng Zhanhai. The details are recorded as follows:

▲ Pseudo-Army Uprising After the battle of Fangzheng, the Liu Baolin Brigade of the pseudo-army was disarmed. It has now been reorganized as the Pseudo-First Mixed Brigade, with Liu still serving as the brigade commander, stationed at Tiandesheng in Shulan. Feng Zhanhai sent a trusted confidant to Liu's defense area to meet with battalion commanders Jiang and Du, explaining to them the great righteousness. Jiang and Du had long intended to revolt, so they contacted the artillery and machine gun companies and others, and on August 2nd, they led more than 1,700 officers and soldiers, carrying 6 machine guns, 4 field guns, and 200,000 rounds of ammunition, and more than 1,000 rounds of artillery shells, to jointly revolt and join Feng Zhanhai. As a result, pseudo-brigade commander Liu Baolin was imprisoned by the Japanese army.

▲ Contacting Righteous Armies At the end of July, the righteous army under Yang Yaogao led 10,000 troops to occupy Zhuhe and continued to advance. On August 9th, they occupied Acheng County. Feng Zhanhai immediately sent the Gong and Yao brigades to advance towards the suburbs of Harbin to make contact with Yang. At the same time, they destroyed the East Road, and traffic between Harbin and Hulan is now cut off.

▲ Attacking Jilin The Wang Delin army has been appearing and disappearing along the Jilin-Dunhua line for a long time, making great contributions to containing the enemy army. Due to a lack of ammunition and supplies, they were unable to engage in a frontal conflict with the Japanese army. Feng Zhanhai recently sent the Tian Brigade and two other detachments and assisted Wang Delin with ammunition and supplies, seeking opportunities to attack Jilin City.

▲ Large-Scale Counter-Offensive Harbin, Wuchang, Shulan, Yushu, and Shuangcheng counties in northern Manchuria have become swamps due to continuous rain. The actions of the Self-Defense Army have been quite difficult, resulting in little development recently. Now that the water level is gradually receding, Feng's troops are actively preparing for a large-scale counter-offensive. A fierce battle will occur soon. (27th)

Shen Honglie's Plan to Expand Naval Factory

Decision to Build a Ship Dock

Presumed Taiping Bay as Dock Site

A communication from Qingdao states that the Northeast Naval Repair Factory was established in Qingdao in the 17th year of the Republic of China. Previously, when the ships belonging to the Northeast Navy were damaged or had mechanical problems, they were mostly repaired by foreign factories, which arbitrarily charged exorbitant prices. The repair costs over the years have been very high. Moreover, all countries in the world that have naval bases have considerable facilities, and repair factories are particularly urgent. Once something happens, we cannot rely on foreigners. Shen Honglie, commander of the Northeast Navy, had this in mind, and thus the naval factory was established. It has been operating for four years, achieving today's results. The evolution of the factory and future construction plans are briefly recorded below:

▲ Factory Evolution In the summer of the 17th year of the Republic, Shen ordered Gao Fenghua, the chief engineer of the Naval Headquarters, to be responsible for establishing the factory and concurrently appointed him as the factory director. He allocated an initial operating fund of 22,000 yuan and purchased old factory machinery from the Japanese Toyosaki Company. He straightened and repaired the original factory site several times before things were on track. The internal organization of the factory consisted of one factory director and two assistant personnel. In order to save expenses, they held concurrent positions and did not receive additional salaries. There were also chief supervisors, technicians, clerks, warehouse managers, and eight foremen, and 32 workers. The monthly salary of the employees amounted to 2,010 yuan, which was paid by the Naval Headquarters. In the 19th year, the budget was increased, with the addition of one foreman to a total of nine, and the workers increased to 56, with the monthly salary amounting to 3,643.5 yuan. In December of the 20th year, a full-time factory director was appointed to take sole responsibility. In February of the 21st year, additional personnel such as technicians and clerks were added, and the budget was increased to 3,957.5 yuan. This is the general overview of the establishment of the factory. Although the shipyard had not yet been built due to funding issues, the various warships could repair all but the underwater parts themselves. The expenses saved in the past three years were considerable. As for the repair project, the budget was first estimated and submitted to the department for approval. After completion, the actual labor and materials used were calculated based on the final calculation, and the repair costs were received. The required cost was very different from that of other factories. Later, as the project increased, the factory site was insufficient for application. After repeated negotiations between the Naval Headquarters and the Qingdao authorities, it was moved to the current factory site in May of the 18th year of the Republic of China (i.e., the old site of the former German torpedo factory). This place has a wide ground, the scale is rough, and it is close to the sea, allowing warships to be parked at the factory dock at any time for construction and repair, which is very convenient for transportation and economical. At the time, Commander Shen believed that the army's radio station was still lacking, so in the 18th year, an electrical engineer was added to the factory's organization to establish a radio factory. In the 19th year, two electrical technicians were added to specialize in long-wave and short-wave radio work. Before long, the Northeast ships and organizations, such as Qingdao, Lushun, Changshan Island, Harbin, Weihaiwei, etc., all installed radio stations. The larger ones can directly connect to Europe and the United States, and the Qingdao central government and various organizations have also requested to be established on their behalf. The Boshan Coal Mining Company also purchased two units, and the

Page 11

Continued Important News

Jiaoji Railway Sifang Park purchased a radio, which was relatively cheap and of good quality, with remarkable results. Later, because the radio factory expanded its organization, it was ordered to be renamed the Naval Radio Station in February of the 21st year. In addition to repairing warships, the factory also engaged in external business. In total, the repair costs of the completed warships were approximately 75,000 yuan in the 18th year, approximately 90,000 yuan in the 19th year, and approximately 130,000 yuan in the 20th year. The repair costs of the completed projects under the Yingzi banner were approximately 1,200 yuan in the 18th year, approximately 3,600 yuan in the 19th year, and approximately 8,000 yuan in the 20th year. Because the project was getting more and more complicated, the number of quota workers was increasingly insufficient. Depending on the situation, dozens to hundreds of temporary workers were hired to supplement the work. As for the purchase of factory assets, in addition to the old factory machinery purchased from the Fongsheng Company, air compressors, slotting machines, washing machines, lathes, gun beds, sawing machines, and many other machines were added, and a timber warehouse, staff dormitory, and blueprint room were built. All the above expenses were allocated as much as possible from the surplus of repair costs, so that such results could be achieved.

▲ Expansion Plan Commander Shen regretted that although the scale of the naval factory was roughly established, the shipyard had not yet been added. Therefore, it was recently decided to build a shipyard, and factory director Gao has been ordered to plan everything. Taiping Bay at the front of the factory has been designated as the dock site. As for the funding for this project, it has been decided to invite merchants to fill the bay outside the dock site. Once completed, it will be put up for lease, and the rental income will be used as construction funds. The Zhengji Shipping Company and major merchants in the city are willing to invest together to achieve this goal. In the future, this matter will not be difficult to realize. After the completion of the dock, not only can ships be repaired, but also new ships can be built. Strengthening national defense, promoting navigation, and prospering the city of Qingdao all depend on this. According to the factory's planned plan, after the dock is completed, it is planned to add a large-scale sand casting factory, a boiler factory, a machine sawmill, a shipbuilding model factory, and a new slipway. The above plans are scheduled to be completed in three years. (August 26)

Value Exceeds Two Million

Fuzhou Correspondence: In Fuzhou, the import of Japanese goods has recently increased significantly. Each time Japanese ships arrive from Taiwan, they are fully loaded with Japanese goods. According to reports from the Min Customs, Japanese goods imported in June and July totaled 10,342 items, weighing 4,054.5 tons, with a value of more than two million yuan. The details and quantities of Japanese goods are listed as follows:

(A) Japanese goods imported in June: (1) Coal: 1,300 tons; (2) Cement: 2,200 bags; (3) Bananas: 1,331 baskets; (4) Seafood: 764 items; (5) Piece goods: 323 items; (6) Sundries (including glass, electrical appliances, enamelware, porcelain, medicine, medical equipment, ironware, rice mills, scientific instruments, generators, Ajinomoto, and various goods from Jiangsu and Guangdong): 385 items; (7) Alcohol: 600 jars. The above totals 5,603 items, weighing 1,915.13 tons.

(B) Japanese goods imported in July: (1) Coal: 1,590 tons; (2) Cement: 1,200 bags; (3) Bananas: 937 baskets; (4) Seafood: 1,197 items; (5) Piece goods: 258 items; (6) Sundries: 221 items; (7) Alcohol: 600 jars; (8) Motor oil: 300 cans; (9) Saccharin: 26 items.

In terms of quantity, June saw 864 more items imported than July. In terms of tonnage, July saw 224 more tons imported than June. As for the sales market, a portion is sold locally, while the rest is shipped to various counties in northern Fujian. Since the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Associations in various circles were disbanded by the provincial government in January of this year, the boycott movement has been neglected, allowing unscrupulous merchants to do as they please. (August 25th)

Records of a Journey West

(10) (1)

Remembering the Song Kilns

After our inspection of the coal mines at the foot of Bai Gong Temple, we took the opportunity to visit the porcelain kilns built during the Song Dynasty. The kilns are located in Chenlu Town, thirty li southeast of Tongguan County. The porcelain produced is as crude as before, with no progress whatsoever. Fortunately, the inconvenient transportation provides some protection; otherwise, they would inevitably be eliminated by natural selection. The clay is extracted from the foothills. After digging holes to extract the clay, the porcelain workers place the mud in a small pool approximately twenty-two feet in diameter. Ox carts are used to drag it around, causing the mud and soil to mix. After some time, the mud settles to the bottom, and the water is released. The mud is then taken from the pool and dragged by mules and horses to the top of the mountain, where it is placed next to the kilns. At this time, there are three workers: one kneading the clay, one forming clay blanks from the kneaded clay, and one making various vessels from the clay blanks, which are then placed in the kiln for firing. There are three types of kilns: large kilns with a length, width, and height of sixteen feet each; medium kilns with a length, width, and height of fourteen feet each; and small kilns with a length, width, and height of four feet each. The kilns produce two types of products: bowls and jars. In terms of bowls, each firing of a small kiln can produce 20,000, a medium kiln 30,000, and a large kiln 40,000. In terms of jars, a large kiln can produce 140 jars, 160 urns, and 80 chuan yu (earthen buckets, etc.). Medium and small kilns do not fire jars. Each worker can make 400 bowls per day. Each kiln requires one type of vessel. Taking three workers as the standard, it takes four months to complete. Loading the clay blanks into the kiln takes about six days, firing takes four days. After firing, it takes about seven or eight days to remove the goods from the kiln in winter, and about eleven or twelve days in summer. Each firing requires 200 baskets of coal for a large kiln, 110 to 120 baskets for a medium kiln, and over 70 baskets for a small kiln. The distribution of compensation is as follows: the two workers who make the clay blanks receive approximately 40% to 50% each, and the remainder goes to the others. For example, if a firing earns 110 yuan, the clay blank makers receive 40 yuan, the clay kneader receives 30 yuan, and the remainder receives 20 yuan each. In total, each kiln can be fired twelve times a year, earning between 240 yuan and 300 yuan each time. The unfired and crude bowls sell for three yuan per hundred, while the fired bowls sell for eight yuan per hundred. Small, unfired four-inch bowls sell for nine jiao per hundred, and two-inch bowls sell for one jiao and five fen per hundred. The glaze used is either white or black. The white glaze comes from Tangjiapu in Fuping County and costs about 1.40 yuan per hundred jin. Each kiln uses 120 jin of glaze per year. The black glaze is local loess.

The kiln area has about three or four hundred households. There are one hundred and twenty to one hundred and thirty kiln caves. The kilns were all built during the Song Dynasty, with seven large kilns, thirty medium kilns, and six or seven small kilns. Each kiln is made of an average of more than 14,000 bricks.

A Brief Account of Tongguan

Tongguan is a small county. The city walls are less than two li in circumference, and it is surrounded by mountains on all sides. Most of the residents live in mountain caves. The area is seventy li from west to east and one hundred and five li from north to south. The population is about five thousand households, or about forty-three thousand people. Their lifestyle is extremely simple. Each person's living expenses are about four or five yuan, which is sufficient. The county government organization only has bureaus for construction, public safety, and finance. There are over one hundred members of the militia and twenty policemen for protection. The sales of foreign goods are almost zero. The entire city only uses fifty boxes of foreign oil per year. There are about thirty shops in the city, each with a capital of no more than three or four hundred yuan.

In terms of education, there is one county normal school, with seventeen students. It only offers one subject, education. Graduation takes two years, and tuition is free. There are two higher primary schools, one inside the city and one in Chenlu Town outside the city. The one inside the city has over one hundred and eighty students and eight teachers. The teachers' salaries are 240 yuan per year, and the principal's is 288 yuan. The one outside the city has fifty-five students and three teachers, with the same salaries. In addition, there are eighty-one elementary schools, with a total of one thousand two hundred and forty students and eighty-one teachers. Their salaries range from 80 yuan to 100 yuan per year. There is one girls' primary school, with thirty-eight students and one principal and one teacher. The principal's salary is 180 yuan per year, and the teacher's is 160 yuan. The education funds are allocated by the Education Fund Custody Office, totaling about eleven thousand and forty yuan per year, including 500 yuan for the normal school and 3,700 yuan for the higher primary schools. The expenses for the elementary schools are borne by the local area. The teachers are all from Shaanxi Province. The curriculum, except for English in the higher primary school, is temporarily based on the primary school curriculum.

Staying Another Day

According to the inspection schedule, we were originally scheduled to depart for Yijun on the morning of the 20th. However, group leader Mr. Hu decided to stay in Tongguan for another day due to the rich mineral resources of Tongguan, in order to inspect other coal mines and not fail the main mission of this trip. However, being here is like being in an area from ancient times. All material backwardness and physical labor are bearable, but the obstructed roads and lack of communication make it impossible to know even the general outline of any earth-shattering events that may be happening in the country. Looking south, I cannot help but feel a long and thoughtful sigh. (Posted from Tongguan on the morning of the 20th)

Continuing News of the Dangerous Seawall Project: The Jinshanzui coastal seawall, during the hurricane on the 23rd of this month, started from the northeast and rotated southwest. The newly built earth and stone works of the second and fourth sections of the west seawall were mostly destroyed, and the cement works of the third section were also severely damaged. The seawall patrol office has summoned the seawall chiefs of each section to guard the seawall day and night and prepare for emergency repairs to prevent accidents. According to reports, this wind and tide is no less than the great wind of August 25th last year. If repairs are not rushed, it will be very dangerous.

Upon hearing the news, the victim Zhang Aibao's family came to Songjiang to care for her in the hospital. Her injuries deteriorated day by day, and she died in the hospital on the 29th. Her husband was very saddened. The murderer's self-inflicted wounds, although not life-threatening, will probably not heal in a short period of time.

Wuxi

Good Autumn Silkworms, Silk Mills Resuming Operations: The silk market has been in a dismal state for years, reaching its lowest point. Recently, in the past two months, the European and American markets have begun to show some activity, and the price of silk cocoons has gradually increased. This year, the autumn silkworms in the four townships of this county are also in excellent condition. The early batches have mostly entered the fourth sleep and begun to eat leaves, and the earliest ones have already begun to spin their cocoons. The late batches are still in the second or third sleep, but the weather has been warm recently, so the silkworms are growing very quickly. A bumper harvest is expected. The silk mills in the city have resumed operations one after another. Large-scale mills outside the South Gate, such as Minfeng Zhenyi, are also preparing to resume operations. Yisheng Silk Mill has scheduled to resume operations on the 4th of next month. This year, the silk cocoon market is taking a tight policy. Last autumn, the rush to buy cocoons led to the bankruptcy of the industry. It is now reported that Zhu Jing'an, the manager of Minfeng Silk Mill, plans to set up fifteen cocoon shops this year, which will open around the 10th of next month, with a price limit of 50 yuan per dan.

Murder and Corpse Removal Case to Undergo Bone Steaming Examination: Jiang Tianzhen, the stepson of Jiang Jufa of Jiangjiatou, Baitaxiang, Fifth District, Wujin County, was murdered by his wife and others. The body was moved to destroy the evidence, and bribes were given to drop the case. After being reported, the procuratorate of the county court has filed a lawsuit according to law. Subsequently, the Henglin Public Security Sixth Sub-bureau arrested the murderer, the deceased's brother, Jiang Fada. Later, Jiangyin also arrested the deceased's mother, Jiang Huangshi, and the original reporter, Xue Aoda, and brought them to the Wujin Procuratorate for interrogation and detention. He then discussed this with the Jiangyin County Government and scheduled the bone steaming examination for September 3rd.

Rugao

The Truth About the Ditch Digging Murder Case: The sensational and bizarre ditch digging murder case has been reported in previous newspapers. In order to seek accuracy, the reporter has learned the truth after several days of investigation. Wang Zijian opened a butcher shop, which suffered heavy losses and could not be sustained. At the time of the closure, he owed Zhang Changshan more than one hundred yuan for pigs. Zhang repeatedly demanded payment, leaving only a little more than twenty yuan unpaid. Around the Ghost Festival, Zhang came to demand payment again, and his words were even more intense. Wang said that he would definitely find a way to repay the debt and would not deduct a single cent. A few days later, Wang tried to find a way and got twenty yuan, which he personally delivered. Zhang insisted on full repayment, and the two sides started arguing. Zhang, with more people and greater strength, tied Wang to a wooden post in the pigsty with a rope, covered him with pig manure, and punched him repeatedly. Wang could only endure this situation and was powerless to resist. After being persuaded by neighbors, he was released. Wang, humiliated and angry, had the thought of death. Taking advantage of the unguarded moment, he hanged himself on a tree in front of Zhang's house. But how the body could reach a tree more than two zhang high is still a question. The county government has now arrested the murderer, Zhang Changshan and his son, for investigation and is summoning Zhang's neighbors, Liu Songling and others, to court for questioning.

Education News

Special Article

Some Humble Opinions on College Student Guidance

Shao Mingjiu

College student guidance occupies a very important position in the administrative organizational system of a university. That goes without saying. But how to achieve practical results is a problem that is not easily solved. In our country, primary and secondary schools are still studying how to improve their guidance organizations and methods. They are willing to accept new and better methods and verify them in practice. Therefore, in recent years, primary and secondary school guidance has indeed shown some progress. Speaking of universities, there is some doubt. To be honest, college student guidance in our country has not made much progress to this day. This is a common phenomenon, not specific to one place or one school, let alone one guidance teacher. I very much hope that universities will work together to study this issue, especially in China, where education is not developed. We must study the organization and methods of college student guidance more carefully so that we can achieve good results and arouse students' attention to guidance. Now I would like to discuss three opinions on the reform of college student guidance with everyone.

(1) Breaking the Director System of Guidance Organization

Currently, there is no standard organization for guidance in general universities in our country, so they can only govern themselves. As far as I know, the names of university guidance organizations generally fall into the following three categories: (1) Director System, (2) Committee System, and (3) Advisor System. Among these organizations, let's not talk about the Committee System and the Advisor System, but only focus on the Director System. I think there are many drawbacks. First, the authority of the guidance director may not be implemented effectively. Second, the guidance office pays too much attention to rules and regulations, and everything is constrained, with little room for flexibility. Third, the guidance office lacks opportunities for contact with the various colleges, so the efficiency of handling affairs is reduced. Fourth, there are few opportunities for contact between teachers and students, so misunderstandings easily arise. Fifth, the emphasis is on the administrative affairs of the guidance office, lacking the promotion of academic research or encouragement of technical inventions. Sixth, it is not appropriate to organize the guidance office alone in terms of funding and talent. The so-called guidance has degenerated into a mechanical undertaking that operates according to regulations under a fixed organization. I believe that the university's guidance organization should be based on the principle of student life, changing the director to instructors, with the number depending on the size of the school's organization. If the organization is simple and the handling of affairs is relatively quick, the drawbacks of too strict organization can be avoided. Therefore, in recent years, universities have gradually tended towards new organizations. (To be continued)

Local News

Advertisements for Private Schools Must Not Confuse the Record-Filing Wording

Advertisements for private schools that have been approved by the Municipal Education Bureau to establish, trial run, or improve are permitted by the Public Utilities Bureau to post announcements free of tax, and are only required to register the Xuan mark at the nearest advertisement management office. However, in recent advertisements for private schools in the city, there are often notes stating "[Education Bureau Record-Filing]". The Public Utilities Bureau found this to be inconsistent with the fixed case. Upon inquiry, the Education Bureau replied that in the future, advertisements for schools with the wording "Record-Filing" or wording inconsistent with the fixed case will not be allowed to be posted to avoid confusion. The Public Utilities Bureau has ordered all advertisement management offices to comply.

Hangkai Football Match Huabu Defeats Biefa to Win the Final

A Ratio of Three to One

In the Hangkai Football Match, Huabu and Biefa Foreign Company held a rematch yesterday at the China Baseball Field. Huabu eliminated Biefa with a score of three to one and won the right to the final. They will compete with Taiping Insurance Company for the championship next Wednesday.

▲ Huabu Scores Three Consecutive Goals in the Second Half The situation on the field was very even at the beginning, with both sides attacking and shooting at each other. However, both sides lost opportunities due to a lack of support. Halfway through the first half, Biefa advanced from the right wing and passed to the center forward. After a melee in front of the goal, center forward Gu Yifei shot the ball into Huabu's goal. Biefa won the first half with a score of one to zero. In the second half, Huabu greatly improved its performance. In less than five minutes, right inside Yao Jiasui broke through the goal, tying the score at one to one. With fifteen minutes remaining, center forward Dong Zhaobin broke the net again, reversing the defeat and winning with a score of two to one. In the last five minutes, right wing Yao Zhilong shot at the goal. The goalkeeper got the ball but lost it again, ending the game with a score of three to one. Huabu played very well in the second half, and its stamina was better than Biefa's.

Swimming Crash Course

Yu Binqi

If we look at it from a physiological point of view, it seems like a reckless and unreasonable act for humans to learn to swim. Everyone understands that fish cannot leave the water. Once they leave the water and are in the air, they will die. Conversely, humans depend entirely on air for survival. If they leave the air and go into the water, wouldn't they die like fish leaving the water and going into the air? But is this really the case? Because humans are the spirit of all things, as long as you can think of it and have the ambition to learn it, you will succeed in anything. Swimming may be a trivial skill, but it is related to life, family, and the nation, and it is of utmost importance. For detailed reasons why this is beneficial to life and the nation, please refer to the telegrams from Binqi and others to the Ministry of Education and the National Sports Conference published in the Shenbao on August 17, 1932, and the Shishi Xinbao on the 18th. This will make it clear that swimming is our urgent task. According to recent statistics, the interest of the Chinese people in swimming seems to be very strong. If you observe the Mingyuan, Hongkou, and Dongya in Shanghai, they are crowded from morning to night, which is a good phenomenon for the sports world. However, although they have a strong determination and are encouraged to bravely learn to swim, without proper training and guidance, they are blindly bumping around like they can't find their way, and it is difficult to get started. Therefore, some people have the will but not the strength and can only sigh at the water. Because my comrades do not abandon me, I often receive letters from various groups asking me to take the time to give guidance. I dare not refuse this kind of appointment and am very happy. Unfortunately, I am too busy and worry that I cannot be everywhere. In addition to apologizing, I offer you a shortcut to swimming here. If you read it carefully, understand it, and practice it in the swimming pool according to my shortcut, I can guarantee that you can swim automatically within one hour. A person who has never been in the water before will probably say that this is a very easy thing when he sees someone swimming. This is really the so-called "watching others carry the burden without feeling the weight." If you go into the water and the water reaches your chest, then your body will float up, and the five internal organs and six lungs in your chest seem to float up as well. Because breathing is short, a state of shortness of breath will appear. For beginners in this situation, how can they fight with the water if they are not guided step by step? Therefore, the basic way to swim is the crawl stroke. Once you have learned the crawl stroke, you have a foundation. After that, if you want to learn other strokes, you can follow the map and solve the problem easily. The practice method of the crawl stroke can be divided into three steps: kicking, stroking, and breathing. When a person enters the water for the first time, he may still feel all kinds of embarrassment when he stands properly. I have already said above that if you ask him to kick his feet, he will really be too scared to try. Why is this? Because the usual way for ordinary people to kick is to grab the pool railing with both hands, stretch their hands straight, and then kick. If you use this method to ask beginners to practice, it is really too profound. I can say assertively that even people with swimming talent cannot stretch and lift their feet straight using this method. If beginners approach the edge of the pool, first grab the stone railing of the pool with their right hand, put their left hand into the water about eight inches from the surface of the water, and hold the pool wall upside down with their fingers pointing down. Then straighten their body into a horizontal line, and then straighten their two feet. Relying on the supporting force of both hands, float the straightened body up, and kick up and down. The movement of kicking only uses the calf to kick, preferably like shivering, which can save a lot of energy. If you grab the stone railing of the pool with your right hand and hold it upside down with your left hand, but your body still cannot float up, then you can use your right hand that is grabbing the stone trough of the swimming pool to lean your arm against the edge of the pool, and the left hand below still holds it upside down. Using this method, even a very fat person can be guaranteed to easily float their body. This secret is what I have learned from years of practice. I have read through Chinese and Western books on swimming and have not mentioned it, so I think it is the most convenient shortcut for beginners to learn to swim in the first step. Kicking requires patience, because it is dull and boring, and it is not good to interrupt it. You must practice it purely and naturally until you can kick without using the strength of your hands.

Local News

Song Cai Flew to Beijing Yesterday Morning

Aircraft Encountered Obstacles

Took Off After Repairs

Song Ziwen, Acting President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, completed his official business in Shanghai and, together with Cai Tingkai, Commander of the 19th Route Army, and secretaries and advisors of the Ministry of Finance, flew to Beijing yesterday morning on Song's own Sikorsky aircraft. Song, Cai, and others were originally scheduled to depart at 6 AM yesterday morning, but were delayed until 10 AM due to engine repairs. At the same time, Cai's original plan to fly directly to Wuhan to meet Chiang after arriving in Beijing was also postponed to this morning. As for this visit of Cai, Minister of Finance Song had agreed to negotiate a total of 700,000 yuan for the financial problems of Fujian. The reorganization of the Fujian Provincial Government will be decided after meeting Chiang.

▲ Delayed Due to Aircraft Damage The Sikorsky aircraft was wiped clean of its components and fuselage by Nai Tuo, a professor at the Aviation School of the Ministry of Military Affairs, and pilot Stenson at around 6 AM yesterday morning. At 6:10 AM, Dr. Young, the American advisor to the Ministry of Finance, arrived alone by car first. The pilot started to crank the right engine first, then the left engine, but it could not be turned due to damage. The pilot Stenson disassembled part of the engine to check and found that the fire door inside was blocked and could not be opened up and down. However, at the same time, due to insufficient electricity, it could not be started even after repairs. At this time, Song and Cai, along with Lu Wenlan and Huang Chundao, secretary of the Ministry of Finance, led several guards and arrived at the scene in three cars. Song and Cai, upon seeing the situation, had no choice but to rest temporarily in the car and wait for the two pilots to repair the aircraft. The two pilots closed the right engine again to focus on repairing the left engine. After three and a half hours, and with the addition of electricity by the Western professor of the Hangzhou Aviation School with a hand-cranked generator, the engine began to move. It was already 9:50 AM. Then, both engines were fully started. Song and Cai then took the newspaper out of the car and boarded the plane with their secretaries. At 10 AM, Nai Tuo and pilot Stenson piloted the aircraft away from the ground.

▲ Going to Wuhan This Morning Those who accompanied Song and Cai included Lu Wenlan, Director of the Songjiang Salt Affairs Audit Sub-Office, Huang Chundao of the Ministry of Finance, and American advisor Dr. Yang Ge, a total of five people. Cai originally planned to fly to Jiujiang and transfer to Hankou to meet Military Committee Chairman Chiang Kai-shek after arriving in Beijing yesterday. However, due to engine damage and prolonged repairs, it was estimated that there would not be enough time after arriving in Beijing, so he temporarily changed his plan to depart from Nanjing this morning, still going to Jiujiang first, and then flying to Hankou to meet Chiang.

▲ Song Discusses Financial Matters When Song Ziwen was about to leave, he talked to a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency about the blockade of the Northeast Customs. The government has no new measures at present and will continue to handle it in the same way as before. Regarding the suspension of payment of the Japanese Gengzi Indemnity, the Japanese had already transferred a part of the Dalian tax once, but the second transfer has not yet arrived. If the Japanese do not continue to remit this tax in the future, whether our side will implement the suspension of payment of the Japanese portion of the Gengzi Indemnity is something that I (Song refers to himself) do not know at present. I completely listen to the government's decision on the Dalian tariff matter. As for acting as the President of the Executive Yuan, because no one is responsible for the Executive Yuan, I have no choice but to act temporarily. The abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan will not be announced for the time being before a decision is made, but the government has decided to proceed with this matter. As for the paper money tax, as mentioned in today's newspapers, the tax has already been received. The tax rate was originally determined by the government to be 2.5%, but now, due to the difficulties of the banking industry, it will be changed to 1.25%. This matter must be decided after I go to Beijing and ask the Legislative Yuan to approve it. The date of return to Shanghai has not been determined, but it will probably not be more than a few days.

▲ Cai Discusses Fujian Matters Furthermore, according to Cai Tingkai, who spoke to a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency, the plan to suppress the bandits in Fujian Province has now been completely decided. After arriving in Beijing this time, he will report to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Wuhan. However, whether this can be achieved immediately after arriving in Beijing today depends on whether there is enough time. As for the financial and reorganization of the provincial government of Fujian, it was not discussed in Shanghai. Although the date of return to Shanghai has not been determined, it will not be long. However, according to Lu Wenlan, who was traveling with Cai, regarding the financial affairs of Fujian, after Cai's meeting with Finance Minister Song in Shanghai, Song had agreed to provide a monthly subsidy of 500,000 yuan, plus a special fund of 200,000 yuan that he had negotiated with Song on behalf of Cai before Cai came to Shanghai. It is estimated that there is still a shortage of 100,000 yuan, but it should not be difficult to raise. The reorganization of the provincial government of Fujian was not discussed in Shanghai, but it is hoped that a decision can be made after meeting with Chiang. Fan Qiwu is likely to agree to take responsibility for the position of Financial Commissioner of Fujian because Fan is one of his own people. Chen Zhenru is determined to go abroad and will not go to Fujian. As for the bandit suppression plan, it has been completely decided and can be reported to Chiang face to face when he meets him.

The Anti-Opium Association Held a National Congress Yesterday

More than 150 Representatives from Various Provinces Arrived

The Meeting Continues Today to Discuss Proposals

The Chinese National Anti-Opium Association held a national congress at the China Society yesterday at 7 PM. Over 150 representatives from anti-opium associations from various regions and from all walks of life gathered together. The meeting commenced at 7:30 PM. During the banquet, Wang Jingqi, Li Denghui, Huang Jiawei, and others from the association delivered opening speeches and reports. Zhang Zhijiang and representatives from anti-opium associations in various regions also gave speeches and reports. The meeting adjourned at 9:30 PM, and it was decided to continue the meeting today to discuss various proposals. The details are recorded separately below.

▲ Representatives Present: Wang Jingqi, President of the Anti-Opium Association; Li Denghui; Huang Jiawei, Executive Director; Zhang Zhijiang, Central Committee Member; Wu Xiaolai from the Shanghai business community (representing Shao Piao); Wu Mai, Director of Publicity for the National Lawyers Association; Lin Kecong from the Shanghai Women's Relief Association; and representatives from anti-opium associations in various regions, including: Hu Jinglu from Suian County, Zhejiang; Ouyang Bokang from Nanjing; Zhong Dacan from Shangyu; Li Fei from Dinghai; Yang Jusong from Zhuji; Yang Zhonggao Dong Sheng; Yang Renrong from Fuzhou; Huang Jinsheng from Yuyao; Pan Shenghua and Zhou Ji from Wenzhou; Tang Qitao from Fenghua; Wu Zhenduo from Shanxi; Wu Zhongmin from Xiashi; Qian Xiaode from Shengxian; Ling Yian from Wuxing; Xu Shu from Chun'an; Tang Bingwen from Haining; Xu Sheng from Xiaoshan; Zhang Renshan from Pei County; Ji Nian from Jiande; Wang Xianglin from Tongxiang; Lin Shize from Xiaofeng; Zheng Dongxiang from Long County; Wang Ziqing from Wuyi; Shen Tu Yu from Tiantai; He Li from Dongyang; Yan Baohang from Liaoning; Li Fengchu from Jiangxi; Zhu Chonghua from Changshu; as well as representatives from the Rickshaw Union, the Shanghai YMCA, the Red Cross, the Shanghai Medical Association, the Rationality Society, and other organizations, totaling over 150 people.

▲ Opening Speech: President Wang Jingqi delivered an opening speech, stating, "Fellow comrades, today marks the opening of the National Anti-Opium Representatives Conference in Shanghai. Comrades who have come from afar braving the summer heat, your enthusiasm and perseverance are deeply appreciated. On behalf of the Chinese National Anti-Opium Association, I extend my warmest welcome. It has been twenty-one years since the founding of the Republic of China. We all share the unspeakable pain of the state of our politics and social customs. Why has China become so corrupt today? Why is the opium scourge so rampant? Why has our international reputation fallen so low? In my personal opinion, it is because in the past twenty-one years, we have focused too much on destructive work and have failed to pay sufficient attention to constructive work, especially psychological reconstruction. The opium problem is a clear manifestation of the psychology of China's undesirable elements. This problem is now inextricably linked to the livelihood of the Chinese people. Diplomacy, finance, transportation, agriculture – all are affected by the opium issue. Other countries use science to alleviate the suffering of the people and increase productivity. However, in our country, it has the opposite effect. Take transportation as an example. In other countries, railways, automobiles, and airplanes facilitate the travel and transportation of goods for the people. But in our country, without new industries or new construction, these advancements only serve to amplify the power of the opium demon. Those who plant, transport, sell, and consume opium are adopting these latest tools to expand their sales and facilitate transportation. Rumors are difficult to verify, but the slogan 'aviation to save the country' is circulating. Some say that aviation is being used solely to transport opium. When will the Chinese revolution succeed? The survival of the Chinese nation depends on the capacity and speed of psychological reconstruction. Among the endeavors of psychological reconstruction, our anti-opium work should serve as a touchstone for testing the resilience of the people and as the strongest and most enduring foundation for national morality. All of us anti-opium comrades should deeply believe in the greatness of our mission and strive to fight for it."

▲ Report on the Process: Li Denghui reported on the proceedings of the congress, stating, "Originally, we planned to hold the congress in Hangzhou, but due to various reasons, we changed the venue to Shanghai. Through the active preparations of the association, overcoming many difficulties, we were able to establish the congress today. Currently, 120 representatives from anti-opium associations in eleven provinces and regions have registered. Representatives from places like Singapore and Taiwan are also participating. We have received over 90 proposals. I hope everyone will work together to achieve the goal of completely eliminating opium."

▲ Speeches from All Sectors: After the report, representatives from anti-opium associations in Liaoning, Singapore, Taiwan, and other places stood up one after another to report on the progress of anti-opium work in their respective regions. Subsequently, Zhang Zhijiang stood up to speak about the scourge of opium, stating that the poison of opium not only subjects China to drug addiction but also endangers the country's survival. This speech garnered enthusiastic applause from the entire audience.

▲ Today's Agenda: Finally, Executive Director Huang Jiawei reported that due to time constraints, the meeting would have to be temporarily adjourned. The meeting will resume tomorrow (i.e., today) at 9 AM and will continue through lunchtime. It will then reconvene in the afternoon. During tomorrow's (30th) meeting, representatives from anti-opium associations in Hebei, Jiangxi, Guangdong, and other provinces, as well as Lin Kecong from the Women's Relief Association and Wu Mai from the National Lawyers Association, will deliver speeches. Various issues will also be discussed. The meeting adjourned at 9:30 PM.

Representatives from Various Organizations in Hongkou Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday

Negotiating Regarding the Actions of the Japanese Outside the Established Order

The various district branches of the Citizens' United Association in Hongkou, as well as the commercial associations of Jiaxing Road, Tongzhou Road, Dongyouheng Road, Hanbury Road, Broadway Road, Yangshupu Road, East and West Huade Road, Yinzhang Road, Suzhou Road, Avenue Edward VII, Haining Road, North Xizang Road, North Jiangxi Road, Chuanbao Road, and other organizations, held an emergency joint meeting the day before to discuss local security issues. They resolved to ban the activities of Japanese ronin organizations such as the Japanese Police Corps in various districts of Hongkou in order to ensure commercial safety. They elected six representatives to petition the municipal government and request negotiations. These representatives went to the Shanghai Municipal Government in Fenglinqiao yesterday morning at 10 AM to petition. The details are recorded separately below.

▲ The Representatives' Petition: The representatives of the organizations, including Zhang Xianfang, Wang Rongtang, Qiu Jialiang, Xing Guxiang, Liu Zhongying, and Zheng Dongshan, submitted a petition to the municipal government, requesting to meet with the mayor. As the mayor was away on official business, Mr. Zhu Weiyao of the Second Section met with them. Wang Rongtang, Zheng Dongshan, Liu Zhongying, Zhang Xianfang, and others spoke in succession, stating the purpose of their petition. In addition to the detailed presentation, the petition included the following points: (A) Shanghai's commerce has suffered immensely since the January 28th Incident. Now, the Japanese Marines are staging demonstrations and patrolling the district, and Japanese soldiers are venturing into the war zone to observe, causing great rumors. It is requested that such actions be strictly rejected in the future to avoid misunderstandings. (B) The local market is operating as usual. Maintaining local order is the responsibility of the Shanghai Municipal Council. Japanese ronin are freely organizing Red Shirt Groups and Japanese Police Corps, parading on the streets and frequently moving around, causing residents to feel fear and preventing them from engaging in business with peace of mind. It is requested that the mayor negotiate with the Japanese side and the Shanghai Municipal Council to promptly ban these groups and maintain local order. (C) At 11 PM on the 10th of this month, over 50 Japanese soldiers in trucks and motorcycles went to the factory of Chen Wanxing on Huasheng Road and Yangzhou Road, injuring several Chinese workers and destroying property in a violent act. It is requested that the mayor promptly initiate serious negotiations, demanding (1) punishment of the perpetrators, (2) compensation, (3) an apology, and (4) guarantees that such barbaric acts will not occur again, in order to appease public anger.

▲ The Municipal Government's Reply: Mr. Zhu Weiyao of the Second Section of the Municipal Government, after hearing the representatives' statements, replied as follows: Regarding point A, he can declare on behalf of the government that the Japanese side has repeatedly requested to visit various districts, but the municipal government has repeatedly rejected these requests. However, the Japanese side has resorted to sophistry. This time, the Public Security Bureau sent police to accompany them on their visits to the war zone. Regarding unauthorized visits, negotiations will certainly be conducted. As for points B and C, they have been detailed in the petition and will be forwarded to the mayor for review and action. The representatives expressed satisfaction with the response and left the government building, nearing noon.

Cannot Tolerate Extreme Patriotic Movements in China

Even More Absurd and Exaggerated than the Previous Announcement to Residents

According to Shishi News Agency, after the Japanese Marine Corps Commander Sugisaka posted the so-called "Announcement to Residents" in the Hongkou area a few days ago, he issued hundreds of mimeographed declarations yesterday, distributing them to Japanese residents in Shanghai. The wording is absurd, and the content is incomprehensible. Here is a translation of the declaration for reference: Declaration: Recently, rumors of renewed fighting have been rampant among Chinese people in Zhabei, Sichuan Road, and other places, causing many to move. Some Japanese residents have also easily believed these rumors, feeling uneasy day and night. This has caused concern among both Chinese and Japanese residents. However, Japan, which has made great sacrifices for the permanent peace of Shanghai, will never take any action that could provoke another conflict. However, covert organizations such as the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Corps, which have sprung up everywhere in China, are creating terrifying rumors to cover up their violent acts. This morning at 10 AM, Ouyang Hong of the Zhabei Fifth District Headquarters of the Chinese Public Security Bureau came to the Marine Corps Headquarters to explain the recent rumors to the Commander. The Commander earnestly stated that if the Chinese side can take responsibility for suppressing all anti-Japanese movements, it would prevent the occurrence of unfortunate incidents. Therefore, he hopes that the Bureau can cooperate closely with the Japanese side to vigorously suppress these anti-Japanese organizations. As for the Japanese authorities stationed in Shanghai, they cannot tolerate these Chinese anti-Japanese conspiracy groups, which lack justice and humanity (?). We are surprised that the Chinese authorities do not suppress those who disrupt public order (?) and damage Sino-Japanese relations (?), allowing them to run rampant everywhere, causing a series of terrifying incidents. This attitude is highly suspicious. As for our Japanese residents in Shanghai, do not believe in rumors and disturb yourselves. You can live and work in peace. If any unfortunate incidents do occur, Japan has the Third Fleet's elite naval force and the Marine Corps' combat-ready land force in Shanghai. All of these forces are more powerful than they were before the January 28th Incident, so there is no need to worry. The Commander will do his best to protect the residents for the sake of their peaceful lives and work. You can all rest assured. This is specially announced.

Inspection to be Held on September 5th

▲ Marine Corps Continues to Arrive: The Japanese Marine Corps in Shanghai has reached 3,000 personnel, with a structure similar to that of the army, including both infantry and artillery. Japanese residents in Shanghai regarded this ship as the last vessel to return home after the Shanghai Battle, and many representatives went to the pier to bid farewell.

The Municipal Committee Sends a Telegram Urging Swift Repairs

The Danjiabang area is also deteriorating daily. If a large autumn tide occurs, a major disaster is inevitable. Committee members have witnessed the current situation and are deeply concerned. A special telegram is sent urging you to swiftly implement the original plan as soon as possible to prevent any eventuality. This is of the utmost urgency."

The Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance Established a Standing Committee Yesterday

Passed the Organizational Outline Principles and Provisionally Elected Temporary Staff

Resolved to Organize an Economic Committee to Raise Funds

The Standing Committee Will Convene its Second Meeting on September 6th Without a Fixed Schedule

After the closing of the Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance Representative Conference, the elected first group of Standing Committee members held the first Standing Committee meeting yesterday at 3 PM at 4 Hong Kong Road. The meeting resolved the organizational outline principles of the Standing Committee, provisionally elected responsible staff, and set the date for the second Standing Committee meeting on September 6th. The details are recorded below.

▲ Standing Committee Members Present: Wu Daquan, Wang Xiaolai, Lu Zhangyuan, Lin Kanghou, Chen Shucheng, Liu Zhanen, Yang Meizhen, Xu Jiying, Chen Liting, Qian Xinzhi, Chen Zheqing, Qin Xiqing, Yan Esheng, Li Kuian, Yu Rongyan, Chen Yaxian, Li Zushen, Yong Jianqiu, Wu Hexuan, Wang Yansong, Pu Xinya, Yu Dichen, Pu Yangshan, Li Gongpu, Lu Quan, Pan Gongzhan, Fu Yueqi, Xu Huaiqing, Liu Guangpei, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Chen Peide, Lin Junbao, and 33 others.

▲ Discussion Details: After the meeting began, Wang Xiaolai was publicly elected as the temporary chairman and Yan Esheng as the temporary secretary. The chairman first introduced each of the attending Standing Committee members. The secretary then reported on the receipt of three letters and telegrams. The meeting then began to discuss the following items: (1) Organizational Outline Principles of the Standing Committee, presented by Wu Daquan, including (A) Duties, (B) Meetings, (C) Organization, and (D) Branches. The attending Standing Committee members discussed each point individually and passed them item by item (the principles are recorded separately). Wu Daquan, Chen Liting, and Yu Rongqiao were then appointed to work with Secretary Yan Esheng to draft the outline based on the passed principles. (2) It was decided that the second Standing Committee meeting would be held on September 6th to discuss the draft outline. Telegrams were immediately sent to Standing Committee members in other cities, urging them to come to Shanghai for the meeting. (3) Before the official staff is elected, Wu Daquan, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Du Yuesheng, and Liu Zhanen will temporarily handle the daily affairs of the General Association. Yan Esheng will be the temporary Secretary-General of the General Association, and Chen Zheqing will be the temporary Accountant of the General Association. (4) The temporary tasks to be handled are as follows: (A) Organizing the resolutions of the General Assembly, (B) Compiling the membership roster and membership application forms, (C) Preparing donation registers. (5) Donation principles were decided upon, and an Economic Committee was organized. Wu Daquan, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiying, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Qian Xinzhi, Qin Xiqing, Chen Liting, and Yang Meizhen were elected as committee members, with Accountant Chen Zheqing as an ex officio member, responsible for convening meetings. (6) The resolutions of each Standing Committee meeting will be printed and distributed to all Standing Committee members for review.

▲ Organizational Outline Principles: The resolved Organizational Outline Principles of the Standing Committee are as follows: (A) Regarding Duties: (1) Standing Committee members may be assigned to handle tasks, (2) The allocation of tasks for handling the affairs of the General Association or branches will be determined by the Standing Committee meeting, (3) In order to ensure speed and agility in handling the affairs of the General Association, five Standing Committee members will be appointed to handle daily affairs, (B) Regarding Meetings: (1) The Standing Committee meeting will be held four times a month as decided by the General Assembly, (2) The location of the Standing Committee meeting will be determined temporarily, (3) The chairman of the Standing Committee meeting can be elected temporarily, (4) There is no fixed schedule for temporary Standing Committee meetings, (C) Regarding Organization: (1) Under the Standing Committee, there will be a Secretariat and an Accounting Office, each with a Secretary-General and an Accountant, appointed by the Standing Committee from among the Standing Committee members, (2) The Secretariat will have a General Affairs Group and a Publicity Group. Committees may be established to study various issues, (D) Regarding Branches: (1) Local branches will be organized by the core members of local legal organizations and must be approved by the General Association, (2) The Standing Committee member of the General Association in the local area will be the ex officio member of the local branch, (3) The purpose of the branch should be based on the purpose of the General Association. If there are any violations, the General Association will suspend its work or cancel it, (4) The expenses of the branch should not be raised locally. A list should be prepared and handled by the General Association.

▲ Drafting Meeting: Immediately after the adjournment of the Standing Committee meeting, the Drafting Committee meeting was convened. Wu Daquan, Chen Liting, Yu Rongqiao, Yan Esheng, and others attended. Chairman Wu Daquan studied the Organizational Outline Principles passed by the Standing Committee meeting and decided that Yan Esheng would draft the initial draft, which would be reviewed by Wu Daquan. The second Drafting Committee meeting will be held on September 1st to pass the draft, which will then be submitted to the Standing Committee for discussion.

▲ Telegrams Sent: Yesterday, the association sent telegrams to the following representatives: Zhou Zuomin and Leng Jiaji in Beiping, Zhang Boling and Zhang Pintai in Tianjin, Zhou Xingtang, Su Taiyu, and Wang Yijian in Hankou, Cai Chang and Ma Wenhui in Hong Kong, Jin Runquan in Hangzhou, and Wu Yifang in Nanjing. The telegram stated that they had been elected as Standing Committee members by the General Assembly and that the Standing Committee meeting was scheduled for September 6th. They were urged to come to Shanghai for the meeting. If this was absolutely impossible, they were asked to entrust a Standing Committee member in Shanghai to represent them in order to facilitate the proceedings. The sender was the Shanghai Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance.

Wu Dingchang, Wu Hexuan, Wen Rongsheng, Xu Jiying, Chen Liting, Wu Zhihao, Li Kuian, Pu Yangshan, Yu Rongqiao, Chen Zheqing, Qian Xinzhi, and over 30 others attended.
