Thorough Investigation of Hand Grenade Casings

For the Use of the 19th Route Army

Zhonghua Ironworks Has Provided Proof

Police Chief Zhang Yaodong of the Sanguantang Police Station in the Second District recently discovered Li Fengren, who was manufacturing bomb casings. Together with the evidence, he was taken to the station for investigation. After interrogation by Chief Zhang, Li Fengren confessed that he owned a sand casting factory. On July 9th, Zhonghua Ironworks ordered 30,000 hemp-tailed hand grenade casings from his factory. He had asked the factory if they had a manufacturing permit, and the factory owner said they did, and that they were intended as a gift for the 19th Route Army. Therefore, he entered into a contract with them to manufacture the casings and dared not do so privately. Chief Zhang, considering that the factory was entrusted to manufacture hand grenade casings, but the district had not received any orders and the factory did not possess any official permits, although Zhonghua Ironworks had provided a letter of proof, still saw the matter of manufacturing munitions as too important to ignore. He decided to transfer Li Fengren, along with two confiscated sample casings and the letter of proof, to the Third Section of the General Bureau for legal action.

Barber Shop Employee Extorting Money Arrested

Huang Hai, a Cantonese man working as an employee at the Yele Barber Shop on Xizang Road, colluded with the fugitive Huang Shengsun and Ouyang Hongkun on the evening of the 24th of this month at 11 PM, pretending to be detectives from the police station. They went to No. 478 Dexing Lane on Peng Road and told the Cantonese woman Xie Lu that her house contained opium, and they were there to search. They found an opium pipe under the bed, but nothing else. They said if she was taken to court, she would be fined 1,000 yuan and sentenced to six months in prison. If she didn't want to go, she could pay 1,000 yuan to settle the matter. If she didn't believe them, the Western detective was at the door. The woman was terrified and, having no such large sum of money, gave them two gold rings worth 80 yuan and an ivory cigarette holder. They arranged to negotiate the next afternoon. When Huang and the others returned, they reduced the extortion to 400 yuan. The woman repeatedly pleaded with them, and they set a date for the payment and left. Several days ago, Bao Tan Feng Qi of the Hongkou Police Station learned of this and arrested Huang Hai, detaining him in the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court. The police lawyer stated that the defendant confessed in the police station that he was planning to smoke opium in a brothel in that lane when he met Huang and Ou, who asked him to enter and was detained. The defendant claimed that Ouyang Hongkun was a detective from the Public Security Bureau and instructed him to wait there. It was a case of mistaken arrest. Judge Shen reviewed the confession and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody for further questioning at a later date.

Head of Sixth District Branch Arrests Principal Offender in Robbery Case

Bi Zhenhua, the head of the Sixth District Branch of the Shanghai West Municipal Public Security Bureau, recently received reports from the police chief of Hongqiao Town that the families of Shen Shaolian, Cheng Zhonglian, Yu Jiatang, and Yu Baoquan in Liujianong, had been robbed one after another. Finally, at the home of Zhang Jinxiang, a Taoist priest on Zhangjialang Road, although they were not robbed, the robbers dared to open fire on the police officers resisting arrest. Director Bi learned that the main criminals in the case, Fang Yousheng and others, were hiding in Qibao Town in western Shanghai. He immediately selected capable police officers Su Jinsheng, Wang Yucai, Chen Qinyu, Zhang Kuiwu, and four others, disguised themselves and waited. They arrested the three thieves, Li Yousheng, Yu Tiangen (also known as Wang Atian or Boss Tian), and Yu Amao. They also confessed that the handgun was given by Xu. Director Bi then dispatched the original group of police officers, wearing plain clothes, to wait at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Avenue Haig in the French Concession at about 8 PM on the evening before last (the 28th). Soon, they saw Xu riding a bicycle from south to north. The police officers bravely stepped forward and arrested him on the spot, sending him to the French Concession police station for temporary detention. Yesterday morning, Director Bi prepared a document and transferred him back to the Sixth District Branch for interrogation. It is said that he confessed that there were still many fugitives at large, and the police have been dispatched separately to strictly arrest them and bring them to justice.

Patient Commits Suicide in Bathroom

On August 2nd, Shen Jingzhi, a 34-year-old man from Hubei, checked himself into the Sacred Heart Hospital in Pudong for treatment of a foot ailment. It has been almost a month and he has not yet recovered, so he remained in the hospital for treatment. Sometime after 7 PM the day before yesterday, for some unknown reason, he went to the bathroom alone and suddenly hung himself from the window with his own belt. Later, Xu Jianhua, a shop owner at the hospital, went to the room to take a bath and saw Shen hanging from the window. Xu was shocked and ran to tell the hospital doctor. They took him down, but his limbs were cold and there was no way to save him. He soon died. The hospital immediately reported to the Yangshupu police station, who ordered detectives to investigate. The body was taken to the forensic center on Fielun Road. Yesterday morning, Zhan Liangce, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, went to the center to examine the body and begin an official inquiry. After hearing Xu Jianhua's account of the situation, Zhan declared that the deceased male, Shen Jingzhi, had indeed committed suicide by hanging. Since there were no relatives to claim the body, the body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial.
